# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

I've created `/workspace/answer.json` with a comprehensive inventory of 18 key files and 31 symbols across the Kubernetes codebase that implement CSI driver integration:

### Key Components Found:

1. **CSI Node Plugin Client** (`pkg/volume/csi/csi_client.go`)
   - Low-level GRPC communication with CSI drivers
   - Methods: `NodePublishVolume()`, `NodeStageVolume()`

2. **CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller** (`pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/`)
   - Creates VolumeAttachment objects
   - Coordinates with reconciler for actual attach/detach operations
   - Checks CSIDriver objects for `attachRequired` capability

3. **CSI Volume Provisioner**
   - Handled by PersistentVolume controller with dynamic provisioning support
   - Marks PVCs with `volume.kubernetes.io/storage-provisioner` annotation
   - Supports CSI migration from in-tree plugins

4. **PersistentVolume Controller CSI Integration** (`pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/`)
   - Bridges CSI operations to core storage API
   - Manages volume lifecycle and handles CSI migration

5. **CSI Node Manager** (`pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/`)
   - Registers CSI drivers on nodes via CSINode objects
   - Communicates driver capabilities to the cluster

6. **Core CSI Plugin** (`pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go`)
   - Entry point for all CSI operations
   - Creates mounders, attachers, block mappers, and expanders

7. **Volume Binding & Scheduler Integration** (`pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/volumebinding/binder.go`)
   - CSI-aware scheduling with in-tree to CSI translation
   - Verifies driver availability on candidate nodes

It provides low-level GRPC communication with CSI drivers deployed on nodes. The client implements methods like `NodePublishVolume()` for mounting volumes and `NodeStageVolume()` for staging operations, directly translating Kubernetes volume operations into CSI gRPC calls.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller\\nThe attach/detach controller is located in `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go` and creates VolumeAttachment objects for volumes requiring attach operations. The `attach_detach_controller.go` coordinates with the reconciler in `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/reconciler/reconciler.go` which orchestrates the actual attach/detach operations. The CSI attacher implementation in `pkg/volume/csi/csi_attacher.go` contains the `Attach()` and `Detach()` methods that execute the actual CSI operations.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Provisioner\\nDynamic provisioning of CSI volumes is coordinated by the PersistentVolume controller in `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go` and `pv_controller_base.go`. This component registers CSI drivers on nodes by populating CSINode objects with driver information. These CSINode objects communicate driver capabilities (like max volume limits) to the cluster, and are used by the attach/detach controller to determine whether volumes can be attached to specific nodes.\\n\\n## Core CSI Plugin\\nThe main CSI plugin implementation in `pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go` registers as a VolumePlugin and acts as the entry point for all CSI operations. The `ProbeVolumePlugins()` function discovers available CSI drivers. The plugin creates mounders via `csi_mounter.go` which handle `SetUpAt()` operations, attachers via `csi_attacher.go`, block mappers via `csi_block.go`, and expanders via `expander.go` for node-side volume expansion.\\n\\n## Volume Binding & Scheduler Integration  \\nThe scheduler's volume binding plugin in `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/volumebinding/binder.go` contains CSI-aware logic including the `tryTranslatePVToCSI()` function that translates in-tree PVs to CSI when migration is enabled. The core architecture consists of:\\n\\n## CSI Node Plugin Client\\nThe CSI node plugin client is implemented in `pkg/volume/csi/csi_client.go` with the `csiDriverClient` struct and `newCsiDriverClient()` function. It provides low-level GRPC communication with CSI drivers deployed on nodes. The client implements methods like `NodePublishVolume()` for mounting volumes and `NodeStageVolume()` for staging operations, directly translating Kubernetes volume operations into CSI gRPC calls.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller\\nThe attach/detach controller is located in `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go` and creates VolumeAttachment objects for volumes requiring attach operations. The controller determines whether attachment is needed by consulting CSIDriver objects via the `CSIDriverLister`, checking the `attachRequired` spec field. The `attach_detach_controller.go` coordinates with the reconciler in `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/reconciler/reconciler.go` which orchestrates the actual attach/detach operations. The CSI attacher implementation in `pkg/volume/csi/csi_attacher.go` contains the `Attach()` and `Detach()` methods that execute the actual CSI operations.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Provisioner\\nDynamic provisioning of CSI volumes is coordinated by the PersistentVolume controller in `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go` and `pv_controller_base.go`. When `EnableDynamicProvisioning` is true and a StorageClass specifies an external provisioner (for CSI drivers), the controller marks PVCs with the `volume.kubernetes.io/storage-provisioner` annotation directing external provisioners to handle the volume creation. The controller handles CSI-specific logic including CSI migration for in-tree plugins translated to CSI via the `InTreeToCSITranslator` interface.\\n\\n## PersistentVolume Controller CSI Integration\\nThe PersistentVolume controller in `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go` bridges CSI operations to the core storage API. It manages the complete lifecycle of PersistentVolumes including deletion and handles CSI migration scenarios where in-tree plugins are migrated to CSI drivers. The controller processes dynamic provisioning requests and coordinates with external provisioners through PersistentVolume objects.\\n\\n## CSI Node Manager\\nThe CSI node info manager in `pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go` implements the `Interface` interface with methods `CreateCSINode()` and `InstallCSIDriver()`. This component registers CSI drivers on nodes by populating CSINode objects with driver information. These CSINode objects communicate driver capabilities (like max volume limits) to the cluster, and are used by the attach/detach controller to determine whether volumes can be attached to specific nodes.\\n\\n## Core CSI Plugin\\nThe main CSI plugin implementation in `pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go` registers as a VolumePlugin and acts as the entry point for all CSI operations. The `ProbeVolumePlugins()` function discovers available CSI drivers. The plugin creates mounders via `csi_mounter.go` which handle `SetUpAt()` operations, attachers via `csi_attacher.go`, block mappers via `csi_block.go`, and expanders via `expander.go` for node-side volume expansion.\\n\\n## Volume Binding & Scheduler Integration  \\nThe scheduler's volume binding plugin in `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/volumebinding/binder.go` contains CSI-aware logic including the `tryTranslatePVToCSI()` function that translates in-tree PVs to CSI when migration is enabled. It uses the `InTreeToCSITranslator` interface to determine migratable volumes and perform translation, consulting CSINode objects to verify driver availability on candidate nodes.\\n\\n## Key Interface Points\\nThe `CSIDriverVolumeHost` interface in `pkg/volume/plugins.go` provides volume plugins access to CSIDriver objects via the `CSIDriverLister()` method. The `AttachDetachVolumeHost` interface extends this for the attach/detach controller specifically, adding access to CSINode and VolumeAttachment listers. The `csiDriverLister` field is initialized from SharedInformerFactory in `pkg/kubelet/volume_host.go` for kubelet and in `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go` for the controller.\"\n}\n",

The controller handles CSI-specific logic including CSI migration for in-tree plugins translated to CSI via the `InTreeToCSITranslator` interface.\\n\\n## PersistentVolume Controller CSI Integration\\nThe PersistentVolume controller in `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go` bridges CSI operations to the core storage API. It manages the complete lifecycle of PersistentVolumes including deletion and handles CSI migration scenarios where in-tree plugins are migrated to CSI drivers. The controller processes dynamic provisioning requests and coordinates with external provisioners through PersistentVolume objects.\\n\\n## CSI Node Manager\\nThe CSI node info manager in `pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go` implements the `Interface` interface with methods `CreateCSINode()` and `InstallCSIDriver()`. This component registers CSI drivers on nodes by populating CSINode objects with driver information. These CSINode objects communicate driver capabilities (like max volume limits) to the cluster, and are used by the attach/detach controller to determine whether volumes can be attached to specific nodes.\\n\\n## Core CSI Plugin\\nThe main CSI plugin implementation in `pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go` registers as a VolumePlugin and acts as the entry point for all CSI operations. The `ProbeVolumePlugins()` function discovers available CSI drivers. The plugin creates mounders via `csi_mounter.go` which handle `SetUpAt()` operations, attachers via `csi_attacher.go`, block mappers via `csi_block.go`, and expanders via `expander.go` for node-side volume expansion.\\n\\n## Volume Binding & Scheduler Integration  \\nThe scheduler's volume binding plugin in `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/volumebinding/binder.go` contains CSI-aware logic including the `tryTranslatePVToCSI()` function that translates in-tree PVs to CSI when migration is enabled. It uses the `InTreeToCSITranslator` interface to determine migratable volumes and perform translation, consulting CSINode objects to verify driver availability on candidate nodes.\\n\\n## Key Interface Points\\nThe `CSIDriverVolumeHost` interface in `pkg/volume/plugins.go` provides volume plugins access to CSIDriver objects via the `CSIDriverLister()` method. The `AttachDetachVolumeHost` interface extends this for the attach/detach controller specifically, adding access to CSINode and VolumeAttachment listers. The `csiDriverLister` field is initialized from SharedInformerFactory in `pkg/kubelet/volume_host.go` for kubelet and in `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go` for the controller.\"\n}\n",
